### `lwjgl3/src/lwjgl3/StartupHelper.java`

- **Package:** `lwjgl3`
- **Primary type:** `class StartupHelper`
- **File length:** 221 lines
- **Intent note (from class doc/comment):** Adds some utilities to ensure that the JVM was started with the {@code -XstartOnFirstThread} argument, which is required on macOS for LWJGL 3 to function. Also helps on Windows when users have names with characters from outside the Latin alphabet, a common cause of startup crashes. <br> <a href= "https://jvm-gaming.org/t/starting-jvm-on-mac-with-xstartonfirstthread-programmatically/57547">Based on this java-gaming.org post by kappa</a> @author damios
- **Internal dependencies (imports):**
  - `program.core.app.Version`
- **Method surface:**
  - `package private StartupHelper()`
  - `public boolean startNewJvmIfRequired(boolean redirectOutput)`
  - `public boolean startNewJvmIfRequired()`
